msg:On a business trip to Wenzhou, I chose the Junting Hotel near Wenzhou South Railway Station. Let me comment on this stay:
Room facilities: The room area is very large. It is initially estimated that the length is more than 9 meters and the width is more than 4 meters. The total area is basically in line with the marked 40 square meters. However, the beauty at the front desk said that this is a room type with an enlarged area, so the 40 square meters marked for the ordinary room type is just Very hydrated? The facilities in the room are great, the space is spacious, the bathroom area is particularly grand, and the experience is great. Standard five-star hotel configuration, no suspense.
Breakfast: The hotel's breakfast area is large and rich in content.
Transportation: The hotel is very close to Wenzhou South Railway Station. There are convenient passages on the second and first floors of the hotel to reach the South Railway Station. It is about 500 to 600 meters away and takes 6-8 minutes to walk. It is very friendly for those who catch the high-speed rail.
The hotel's deposit refund efficiency is pretty good, one hour after check-out
Let‚Äôs talk about some flaws and poor experience: First of all, you can only add 3 bottles of mineral water, and it is still a 350ml small bottle of Chunyue, which is very cheap and low-end water. However, you will be charged for more than 3 bottles, which is a bit tricky! The socket in the room seemed to have popped out. . . The sewer in the bathroom is not very good. When showering, the water flows very slowly and fills up easily. You basically have to step on the water while taking a shower. . . There is no coffee provided in the five-star hotel room, only simple tea bags. . . Hotel TVs opened in 2020 do not have screen projection functions and have a small number of movies. However, given the spacious size of the room and the high-quality bedding, I still give it full marks.
